           <h2 style="text-align: center;">
            Welcome to Yellow Door Lets
            <sup>
             ®
            </sup>
           </h2>
           <h3 style="text-align: center;">
            Quality Student Housing in Lancaster Since 1983
           </h3>
           <h3 style="text-align: center;">
            Yellow Door Lets
            <sup>
             ®
            </sup>
            are proud to announce we are now part of the
            <a href="https://www.lancasteruniversityhomes.co.uk/" target="_blank">
             Lancaster University Homes accredited scheme.
            </a>
            <a href="https://www.lancasteruniversityhomes.co.uk/" target="_blank">
             <img alt="Lancaster University Homes" height="27" src="https://www.yellowdoorlets.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/banner-bg-e1478513369377.png" style="vertical-align: bottom;" width="72"/>
            </a>
           </h3>
           <p style="text-align: center;">
            Yellow Door Lets® own the largest number of
            <a href="https://www.yellowdoorlets.co.uk/houses/">
             student houses in Lancaster
            </a>
            and all are in great locations near Cumbria University or near bus stops for
            <a href="http://www.lancaster.ac.uk/" target="_blank">
             Lancaster University
            </a>
            . If you’re looking for quality, affordable and brilliantly situated student accommodation, why not take a look at the range of
            <a href="/houses/">
             houses which we offer
            </a>
            ? In doing so, you could save yourself up to £30 per week when compared to living on campus. All of our student accommodation in Lancaster include free contents insurance, FREE UNLIMITED FIBRE BROADBAND UP TO 80Mbps and even a TV licence. Wherever possible double or 3/4 beds are provided, FREE GAS AND ELECTRICITY and no water rates to pay.
           </p>

           <h5 style="text-align: left;">
            Finding the right student accommodation in Lancaster.
           </h5>
           <p style="text-align: left;">
            Searching for the right student accommodation in Lancaster with Yellow Door Lets has never been easier. From our
            <a href="/search-houses/">
             search page
            </a>
            , simply select the number rooms you require, the location best suited and we’ll do the rest. You will be presented with a list of available student houses or rooms in Lancaster. From there, it’s up to you. Get in touch and we can arrange a viewing for your perfect student accommodation.  Call us on 07774 920816 or email
            <a href="mailto:info@yellowdoorlets.co.uk">
             info@yellowdoorlets.co.uk
            </a>
           </p>
